
namespace = flavor_feiten

######################################
# State sponsored whaling expedition #
######################################

# Set off
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.1
	title = flavor_feiten.1.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.1.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
				duration = -1
			}
			set_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition
		}
	}

	# Letsago
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.1.a
		tooltip = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.2 days = 180 random = 60 } }
	}
}

# Bored at sea
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.2
	title = flavor_feiten.2.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.2.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	# Adm (its candle wax/lantern oil)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.a
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
	# Dip (its Ambergris)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.b
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip
		add_dip_power = -50
	}
	# Mil (its baleen and its myriad uses)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.c
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil
		add_mil_power = -50
	}
	# We got no time to waste on these friviolities
	option = { name = flavor_feiten.2.d }
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_feiten.3
				days = 120 random = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

# The hunt begins
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.3
	title = flavor_feiten.3.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.3.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	# Volunteer for one of the boats
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.3.a
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 5 }
		add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 5 }
		random_list = {
			# Injured
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = "[Root.Monarch.GetName] gets injured..."
				set_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale
			}
			# You're fine
			50 = { set_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed }
		}
	}
	# Sit back and watch... carefully
	option = { name = flavor_feiten.3.b }

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.4 } }
}

# Hunt results
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.4
	title = flavor_feiten.4.title
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale }
		desc = flavor_feiten.4.descInjured
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed }
		desc = flavor_feiten.4.descMobyDicked # No I haven't read the book :P
	}
	desc = flavor_feiten.4.satBack
	
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.4.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed }
			add_prestige_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 25 }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = feiten_whale_slayer duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = feiten_whaling_injury duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.5 days = 120 random = 30 } }
}

# Bored at sea redux
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.5
	title = flavor_feiten.5.title
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.oil
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
	}
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.ambergis
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
	}
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.baleen
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
	}
	desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
		change_adm = 1
		4878 = { # 
			change_trade_goods = naval_supplies
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_lantern_oil
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
		change_dip = 1
		4878 = {
			change_trade_goods = incense
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_ambergris
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
		change_mil = 1
		4878 = {
			change_trade_goods = ivory
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_baleen
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
		}
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_whale_meat
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.6 days = 60 random = 10 } }
}

# Triumphant return
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.6
	title = flavor_feiten.6.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.6.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.6.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
		clr_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition
	}
}

# Our guy dies during the trip

	desc = flavor_feiten.7.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Ah, well shit

		name = flavor_feiten.7.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
	}
}

# Short balloon research chain #

# Intro/start
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.30
	title = flavor_feiten.30.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.30.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Favor Xiao Yang's theory and research
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.30.a
		set_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_church
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}

	# Favor Da Jin's theory and research
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.30.b
		set_country_flag = da_jin_favored
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_eunuchs
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.31 days = 1095 random = 180 } } }
}

# Struggles
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.31
	title = flavor_feiten.31.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.31.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes


	# Delays? Keep at it champ
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.a
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 1825 random = 365 }
	}

	# Moar powah!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.b
		add_dip_power = -25
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_adm_power = -25
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 365 random = 90 }
	}

	# Have them work together
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.c
		trigger = {
			is_advisor_employed = 6969
			is_advisor_employed = 9696
		}
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 10 }
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 365 random = 90 }
		clr_country_flag = da_jin_favored
		clr_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored
		set_country_flag = balloon_research_teamwork
	}
}

# Prototype complete!
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.32
	title = flavor_feiten.32.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.32.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.32.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_starting_balloon_research
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = balloon_research_teamwork }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_teamwork_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = da_jin_favored }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_da_jin_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_xiao_yang_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
	}
}
#########################################
# The rise and decline of whale hunting #
#########################################
# Development of 'group' fishing
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.40
	title = flavor_feiten.40.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.40.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Hell yeah brother
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.40.a
		4878 = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_province_modifier
				feiten_lantern_oil = {
					remove_province_modifier = feiten_lantern_oil
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_lantern_oil_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				feiten_ambergris = {
					remove_province_modifier = feiten_ambergris
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_ambergris_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				feiten_baleen = {
					remove_province_modifier = feiten_baleen
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_baleen_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				feiten_whale_meat_upgraded = {
					remove_province_modifier = feiten_whale_meat_upgraded
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_whale_meat_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Collapse of fisheries
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.41
	title = flavor_feiten.41.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.41.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Just... tell them to chill for a bit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.41.a
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 7300
			}
			set_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action
		}
	}

	# Commission a commitee to figure out what to do/plan better
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.41.b
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
}

# Development of modern harpoon guns and steamboats
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.42
	title = flavor_feiten.42.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.42.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We should pump the brakes a bit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.42.a
		4878 = { add_base_production = 2 }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			loyalty = -10
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.43 days = 7300 random = 1825 } }
	}

	# Full steam ahead!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.42.a
		4878 = { add_base_production = 5 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.43 days = 1825 random = 365 } }
	}
}

# Advocates of the traditional methods get angry
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.43
	title = flavor_feiten.43.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.43.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Give in to their demands
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.43.a
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 10 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.44 days = 18250 random = 3650 } }
	}

	# The future is now, old man!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.43.b
		add_yearly_sailors = -2
		4878 = { add_unrest = 10 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.44 days = 7300 random = 1825 } }
	}
}

# Collapse redux
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.44
	title = flavor_feiten.44.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.44.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Oof
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.44.a
		4878 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse_drastic
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

####################################
# Bombs of Tianlou events n' stuff #
####################################
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.70
	title = flavor_feiten.70.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.70.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.70.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_bombs_over_tianlou_mod
			duration = 1825
		}
		4871 = {
			change_siege = 10
			add_devastation = 50
			add_base_tax = -1
			add_base_production = -1
			add_base_manpower = -1
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = damaged_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = derelict_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

######################
# Skyport post stuff #
######################

# Build a skyport in an owned province
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.100
	title = flavor_feiten.100.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.100.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Pick a bunch of locations
		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag
				save_event_target_as = feitenSkyportTarget1
			}
		}

		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag
				save_event_target_as = feitenSkyportTarget2
			}
		}

		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag
				save_event_target_as = feitenSkyportTarget3
			}
		}

		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}

	immediate = {
		# Pick a bunch of locations

					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1

				}

			}
		}

# Dismantle a skyport in a province
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.102
	title = flavor_feiten.102.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.102.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2
			}

# Skyport menu
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.104
	title = flavor_feiten.104.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.104.desc
	picture = FEITEN_SKYPORT_GUI_PIC_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	# Issue Silken Council Proclamation
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.b
		custom_tooltip = silkenProclamationInfoTT
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationMarketplaceOfIdeas
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationOpenDoor
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationAirliftsAndDefence
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationNone
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.106 } }
		}
	}

	# Construct Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				any_trade_node = {
					all_trade_node_member_province = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
					}
					any_trade_node_member_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.100 }
		}
		# Construct TT
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = cannotConstructSkyportTT
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.105 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportNotBelowCapTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportBelowCapTT }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_trade_node = {
							all_trade_node_member_province = {
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
							}
							any_trade_node_member_province = {
								owned_by = ROOT
								province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
								NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsNotFulfilledTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsFulfilledTT }
		}
	}

	# Dismantle Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.d
		custom_tooltip = "The following provinces have Skyports that can be dismantled:"
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = "Y[This.GetName]!"
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.102 } }
	}

	# Monthly Skyport Duty Breakdown
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.e
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.105 } }
		tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = feitenSkypostDutyEff value = 100 } }
				5381 = { if = { limit = { any_trade_node_member_province = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod } } add_trade_node_income = 1.0 custom_tooltip = "" } }
				5202 = { if = { limit = { any_trade_node_member_province = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod } } add_trade_node_income = 1.0 custom_tooltip = "" } }
				5179 = { if = { limit = { any_trade_node_member_province = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod } } add_trade_node_income = 1.0 custom_tooltip = "" } }
				5315 = { if = { limit = { any_trade_node_member_province = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod } } add_trade_node_income = 1.0 custom_tooltip = "" } }
				5312 = { if = { limit = { any_trade_node_member_province = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod } } add_trade_node_income = 1.0 custom_tooltip = "" } }

		}

		else = {

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.106 } }
		}
	}

	# Construct Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				any_trade_node = {
					all_trade_node_member_province = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
					}
					any_trade_node_member_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.100 }
		}
		# Construct TT
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = cannotConstructSkyportTT
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportNotBelowCapTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportBelowCapTT }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_trade_node = {
							all_trade_node_member_province = {
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
							}
							any_trade_node_member_province = {
								owned_by = ROOT
								province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
								NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsNotFulfilledTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsFulfilledTT }
		}
	}

# Convene Silken Council
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.106
	title = flavor_feiten.106.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.106.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# the admin one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.a
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = "Issuing this Proclamation will cost Y50! adm per province.\nThe following provinces will gain G+1! icon_tax_in_text.\nThe following provinces will get the following modifier for 10 years:\nADD HERE\n"
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = "Y[This.GetName]!"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_tax = 1
				ROOT = { add_adm_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# the dip one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.b
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = "Issuing this Proclamation will cost Y50! dip per province.\nThe following provinces will gain G+1! icon_production_in_text.\nThe following provinces will get the following modifier for 10 years:\nADD HERE\n"
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = "Y[This.GetName]!"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_production = 1
				ROOT = { add_dip_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# the mil one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.c
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = "Issuing this Proclamation will cost Y50! mil per province.\nThe following provinces will gain G+1! icon_manpower_in_text.\nThe following provinces will get the following modifier for 10 years:\nADD HERE\n"
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = "Y[This.GetName]!"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_manpower = 1
				ROOT = { add_mil_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# NEVERMIND
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.d
		custom_tooltip = "Back to Skyport menu"
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } } }
}

# Pick settler policy
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.200
	title = flavor_feiten.200.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.200.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Settle impressed sailors
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.200.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_impressed_settlers
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	# First dibs/focus with merchants/trade
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.200.b
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_trade_focus
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

# Box Jellyfish event
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.201
	title = flavor_feiten.201.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.201.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Load em' up
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.201.a
		random_hired_mercenary_company = {
			limit = { template = merc_feiten_box_jellyfish }
			location = {
				while = {
					limit = {
						num_of_units_in_province = {
							who = ROOT
							type = marine_infantry
							amount = 1
						}
					}
					kill_units = {
						who = ROOT
						type = marine_infantry
						amount = 1
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numMarinesOnBoxJelly value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_box_jelly_cooldown
			duration = 30
		}
	}

	# Pop em' out
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.201.b
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = numMarinesOnBoxJelly
					value = 1
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = { which = numMarinesOnBoxJelly value = 1 }
			random_hired_mercenary_company = {
				limit = { template = merc_feiten_box_jellyfish }
				location = {
					marine_infantry = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_box_jelly_cooldown
			duration = 30
		}
	}
	
	# Nevermind
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.201.c
		highlight = yes
	}
}

# Lightning Jellyfish event
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.202
	title = flavor_feiten.202.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.202.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Let 'er rip
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.202.a
		random_hired_mercenary_company = {
			limit = { template = merc_feiten_lightning_jellyfish }
			location = {
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { war_with = ROOT } }
					change_controller = ROOT
					add_devastation = 50
					random_list = {
						1 = { add_base_production = -1 }
						1 = { add_base_tax = -1 }
						1 = { add_base_manpower = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Nevermind
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.202.b
		highlight = yes
	}
}
